    "tickets_link": "https://www.billetweb.fr/english-food-collage-online-with-anna&multi=11155&margin=no_margin&color=f71920&parent=fresquealimentation&margin=no_margin&color=f71920",
    "description": "Workshop Description\nThe Food Collage workshop is a fun and educational session designed to guide participants toward more sustainable eating habits and to raise awareness of the impacts of their food choices (environment, biodiversity, health, and territorial resilience).\nThe workshop is adaptable and also available in an online version!\nThe workshop is inspired by its big sister, the Climate Fresk, but having done it beforehand is not a prerequisite! (click HERE to participate)\nThe workshop is based on collective intelligence. The facilitator is there to ensure everything runs smoothly, answer questions, and guide the process\u2014but the participants are the ones doing the work!\nThe Reflection phase is based on 40 cards divided into 5 sets, which participants arrange by linking causes and consequences with arrows.\nThe workshop encourages taking action (eating local food, seasonal products, a more plant-based diet, etc.).\nIt is based on scientific and recognized sources (FAO, IPCC, ADEME, etc.).\nThe workshop is aimed at adults (a specific junior version also exists), whether experts or beginners on the topic, already committed\u2014or not\u2014to more sustainable eating. In short, the workshop is for anyone who wants to better understand what they eat! No prerequisites are required to participate.\nWorkshop Format\nThe workshop lasts 3 hours and is divided into several stages:\nStart (30 min): icebreaker, introductions of participants and the facilitator, presentation of the workshop, etc.\nReflection (1h15): exploration of the causes and consequences of our consumption habits on the climate, biodiversity, health, and food system resilience.\nSolutions (30 min): what solutions can we implement right now, at our own scale, to move toward more sustainable food? What are their consequences?\nActions (30 min): choosing one individual action and one collective action to move toward more sustainable food systems, and anticipating possible challenges or barriers.\nDebrief (15 min): feedback on the workshop, final advice, and discussion on what comes next after the workshop.\nBelieve us, it goes by (very) quickly!\nPractical Information\nMaterials\nYou don\u2019t need anything! :)\nWant to organize a workshop for your organization?\nhttps://forms.gle/ZhiyKGgcQmMYQxMt7\nContacts\nWebsite: http://fresquealimentation.org\nLinkedIn page\nFacebook page",

Bref, l'atelier s'adresse \u00e0 quiconque souhaite comprendre ce qu'il.elle mange ! Aucun pr\u00e9requis n'est demand\u00e9 pour faire l'atelier !\nD\u00e9roul\u00e9\nL\u2019atelier dure environ 3h et se d\u00e9coupe en plusieurs \u00e9tapes :\nD\u00e9marrage (30 min) : icebreaker, pr\u00e9sentation des participant.e.s, de l\u2019animateur.rice, de l\u2019atelier, \u2026\nR\u00e9flexion (1h15) : \u00e9tude des causes et cons\u00e9quences de nos consommations sur le climat, la biodiversit\u00e9, la sant\u00e9 et la r\u00e9silience alimentaire\nSolutions (30 min) : quelles solutions pouvons-nous mettre en place d\u00e8s maintenant \u00e0 notre \u00e9chelle pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable ? Quelles sont leurs cons\u00e9quences ?\nActions (30 min) : choix d\u2019une action individuelle et une action collective pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable et anticipation des difficult\u00e9s/freins qui pourraient \u00eatre rencontr\u00e9s\nD\u00e9brief (15 min) : retours sur l\u2019atelier, derniers conseils, quelle suite donner \u00e0 l\u2019atelier, ...\nCroyez-nous, \u00e7a passe (tr\u00e8s) vite !\nInfos pratiques\nMat\u00e9riel\nVous aurez simplement besoin d\u2019un ordinateur, d\u2019un micro et d\u2019une connexion internet suffisante pour pouvoir \u00e9changer avec les autres participant.e.s. Aucun pr\u00e9requis n'est demand\u00e9 pour faire l'atelier !\nD\u00e9roul\u00e9\nL\u2019atelier dure environ 3h et se d\u00e9coupe en plusieurs \u00e9tapes :\nD\u00e9marrage (30 min) : icebreaker, pr\u00e9sentation des participant.e.s, de l\u2019animateur.rice, de l\u2019atelier, \u2026\nR\u00e9flexion (1h15) : \u00e9tude des causes et cons\u00e9quences de nos consommations sur le climat, la biodiversit\u00e9, la sant\u00e9 et la r\u00e9silience alimentaire\nSolutions (30 min) : quelles solutions pouvons-nous mettre en place d\u00e8s maintenant \u00e0 notre \u00e9chelle pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable ? Quelles sont leurs cons\u00e9quences ?\nActions (30 min) : choix d\u2019une action individuelle et une action collective pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable et anticipation des difficult\u00e9s/freins qui pourraient \u00eatre rencontr\u00e9s\nD\u00e9brief (15 min) : retours sur l\u2019atelier, derniers conseils, quelle suite donner \u00e0 l\u2019atelier, ...\nCroyez-nous, \u00e7a passe (tr\u00e8s) vite !\nInfos pratiques\nMat\u00e9riel\nVous aurez simplement besoin d\u2019un ordinateur, d\u2019un micro et d\u2019une connexion internet suffisante pour pouvoir \u00e9changer avec les autres participant.e.s. Si vous avez une souris \u00e0 molette c\u2019est l\u2019id\u00e9al, sinon que \u00e7a soit avec le trackpad ou une souris classique, l\u2019atelier peut se faire sans probl\u00e8me !\nConnexion \u00e0 la visio\nUn lien vers Zoom vous est communiqu\u00e9 dans le billet et vous sera \u00e9galement rappel\u00e9 par mail juste avant l\u2019atelier ! If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

How can companies evolve their business models?\nTo discover the answers to these and many other questions, come and take part in a workshop of the Circular Economy Collage. The workshop covers topics such as climate change, biodiversity loss, resource scarcity and pollution generated by human activities and enables you to identify concrete courses of action!\nAbout the workshop\nThe Circular Economy Collage is a stimulating, group-based workshop founded on scientific information, which enables participants to grasp the limits of our existing global \u201clinear\u201d economy and understand the opportunities offered by the circular economy. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

The workshop covers topics such as climate change, biodiversity loss, resource scarcity and pollution generated by human activities and enables you to identify concrete courses of action!About the workshopThe Circular Economy Collage is a stimulating, group-based workshop founded on scientific information, which enables participants to grasp the limits of our existing global \u201clinear\u201d economy and understand the opportunities offered by the circular economy. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The online workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.Our online Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools. For our online public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.Benefits of the workshopHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",
